# Reasoning Failure Modes

This reference lists the failure patterns that most often cause an agent to sound confident while being wrong.

## Premature Certainty

Premature certainty happens when a plausible explanation becomes the working truth before it is tested. The recovery move is to write the claim as a hypothesis and ask what observation would disprove it.

## Local Fixation

Local fixation happens when the visible failing line receives all attention while the actual cause is upstream. Trace the data into the line before editing the line itself.

## Tool Output Skimming

Tool output skimming happens when only the first or last lines are read. Stack traces, compiler errors, and test failures often contain the key detail in the middle.

## Scope Creep

Scope creep happens when the agent starts improving nearby code because it is visible. Keep a separate note for follow-up improvements and finish the requested change first.

## Recovery Triggers

Restart the reasoning process when:

- The same fix fails twice.
- The code behaves differently than predicted.
- The explanation requires ignoring an observed fact.
- The diff grows beyond the original mental model.
- Verification passes only indirectly.

When any trigger fires, stop editing and rebuild the hypothesis tree from observed evidence.
